 What Happens Cardiac arrest is a cardiac arrest that suddenly stops working
 ye koi lambii beemaari kaa hissaa nahin he isliye ye dil se judi bimariyon main sabase khatarnaak mana jaataa he
 Because of this, your heart can be weak due to heart attack
 People often consider it to be a heart attack
 magar ye usase alag he
 Experts state that cardiac arrest occurs when the heart stops pumping blood around the body
 medical turm main kahen to heart atake circulatory samasya he jabaki cardiyak atake, electric conduction kii gadabadi kii vajah se hota he
 If there is pain in the sense of heart pain, it is not necessary that it is happening only during a heart attack
 doctors ke mutabik, aisa heart bern yaa cardiyak atake ke kaaran bhi ho saktaa he
 Now the calculator will tell how stressed you are, know how
 
 
 kyon he khatarnaccardiyak arest main dil kaa blad cirkulation puri tarah se band ho jaataa he
 This affects the heartbeat as ventricular fibrillation occurs inside the heart
 isliye cardiyak arest main kuch hi minuton main maut ho sakati he
 What are the symptoms
 Cardiac arrest is so sudden
 haalanki jinhen dil kii beemaari hoti he unamem cardiyak arest kii ashanka zyada hoti he
 Occasionally prior to cardiac arrest, there may be chest pain, trouble breathing, palpitations, dizziness, fainting, fatigue, or blackout
 kaise hota he ilajiske ilaaj ke liye marij ko cardeopulmonary resstiseshan (seepiaar) diya jaataa he, jisase uski dil kii dhadkan ko regular kiya ja sake
 Its patients try to make the heart beat regular by giving them an electric shock with a 'defibrillator'

 Smartphones have become an unbreakable part of our lives
 haath main smartphone na ho to lagata he ki koi bahut jaruri cheez chhot gai he
 It is a habit and necessity to see mobile once every five-ten minutes
 par smartphone ke is kadar istemaal kaa sabase bura asar hamaari ankhon par padataa he
 If you are also among those who look at the screen of your smartphone 150 times or more in a day, then your eyes may have to pay for it
 bahut lambey samay tak mobile, tablet or laptop kii screen dekhne se ankhon main jalan, thakaan or dhundhala najar aane kii samasya ho sakati he
 Apart from this, spending too much time on screen also dries up the eyes
 agar aapako bhi ankhon se judi ye pareshaaniyaan hai to ye aasaan se upaay aapkorahat dilaa sakate hai
 1
 kuch-kuch der main palkon ko jhapakate rahane se ankhon kii nami bani rahati he or jalan nahin hoti
 2
 apane smartphone kii screen par protector film lagaaein
 You can also use an anti-reflecting coat if you want
 3
 Take a break from your smartphone
 bhale hi ye aapako sunne main atapata lage lekin aapaki ankhon ke liye ye bahut phydemand rahegaa
 Try to see the smartphone once every 20 minutes and only for 20 seconds
 4
 Adjust the brightness of your smartphone correctly
 screen na to bahut adhik brit honi chahie or na hi bahut adhik dark
 5
 aapke smartphone ke text kaa sies or contrast sahi hona chahie
 This will make it easier to read and less emphasis on the eyes
 6
 Always keep mobile screen clean
 gande screen se focus banane main dikkat hoti he or isse ankhon par jor padsakta he
 7
 samartphone ko uchit duuri par rakhana bahut jaruri he
 Type or read anything by keeping the smartphone at a distance of 8 inches
